2025-06-23 21:12:28.561 +05:30 [INF] Executed DbCommand (7ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT p."Id", p."Content", p."IsDeleted", p."Slug", p."Status", p."Title", p."UserEmail", u."Email", s."CategoriesId", s."PostsId", s."Id", s."Name", u."Bio", u."CreatedAt", u."IsDeleted", u."IsSuspended", u."Location", u."Name", u."PasswordHash", u."ProfileImage", u."Role", u."Status", u."SuspendedUntil", u."SuspensionReason", u."Website"
FROM "Posts" AS p
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON p."UserEmail" = u."Email"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p0."CategoriesId", p0."PostsId", c."Id", c."Name"
    FROM "PostCategories" AS p0
    INNER JOIN "Categories" AS c ON p0."CategoriesId" = c."Id"
) AS s ON p."Id" = s."PostsId"
WHERE NOT (p."IsDeleted")
ORDER BY p."Id", u."Email", s."CategoriesId", s."PostsId"

SELECT p."Id", p."Content", p."IsDeleted", p."Slug", p."Status", p."Title", p."UserEmail", u."Email", s."CategoriesId", s."PostsId", s."Id", s."Name", u."Bio", u."CreatedAt", u."IsDeleted", u."IsSuspended", u."Location", u."Name", u."PasswordHash", u."ProfileImage", u."Role", u."Status", u."SuspendedUntil", u."SuspensionReason", u."Website", i."Id", i."Content", i."IsDeleted", i."Name", i."PostId", i."UploadedAt", c0."Id", c0."Content", c0."CreatedAt", c0."IsDeleted", c0."PostId", c0."Status", c0."UserEmail"
FROM "Posts" AS p
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON p."UserEmail" = u."Email"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT p0."CategoriesId", p0."PostsId", c."Id", c."Name"
    FROM "PostCategories" AS p0
    INNER JOIN "Categories" AS c ON p0."CategoriesId" = c."Id"
) AS s ON p."Id" = s."PostsId"
LEFT JOIN "Images" AS i ON p."Id" = i."PostId"
LEFT JOIN "Comments" AS c0 ON p."Id" = c0."PostId"
WHERE NOT (p."IsDeleted")
ORDER BY p."Id", u."Email", s."CategoriesId", s."PostsId", s."Id", i."Id"
